The ventrolateral branch forms postsynaptic terminals in the AMMC zone B (Matsuo et al., 2016). The dorsal branch bifurcates in the ipsilateral epaulette, projecting above the esophagus, to form presynaptic terminals both the ipsilateral and the contralateral wedge (Matsuo et al., 2016).
